        (PP (IN for)
          (NP
            (NP (NN instance) (DT the) (NN memory))
            (PP (IN of)
              (NP
                (NP (DT some) (JJ leading) (NN man))
                (PP (IN of)
                  (NP (DT the) (NN past)))))))))
    (. .)))
